PS C:\Users\Administrator.ADATUM> $list = @("name","city","office","department")
get-aduser -filter 'city -like "london"' -SearchBase "OU=IT,DC=Adatum,DC=com" -Properties $list | 
sort Givenname | 
select $list |
ConvertTo-Html |
out-file toto.html

.\toto.html
PS C:\Users\Administrator.ADATUM> 
$Header = @"
<style>
TABLE {border-width: 1px; border-style: solid; border-color: black; border-collapse: collapse;}
TD {border-width: 1px; padding: 3px; border-style: solid; border-color: black;}
</style>
"@

$list = @("name","city","office","department")
get-aduser -filter 'city -like "london"' -SearchBase "OU=IT,DC=Adatum,DC=com" -Properties $list | 
sort Givenname | 
select $list |
ConvertTo-Html -Head $Header |
out-file toto.html

.\toto.html
